example8-list compiled
example8-list manage permit ip any any 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit icmp any any echo 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit icmp any any echo-reply 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit icmp any any time-exceeded 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit icmp any any unreachable 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit udp any object-group dns-intranet eq domain 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit ip object-group rasvpn-emp object-group intranets 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit ip object-group rasvpn-emp 192.168.0.120 255.255.255.0 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit udp object-group rasvpn-infra object-group nsm-servers object-group grp-trap-syslog 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit udp object-group rasvpn-infra object-group radius-servers eq radius-acct 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit udp object-group rasvpn-infra object-group radius-servers eq radius 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit udp object-group rasvpn-infra object-group nsm-servers eq tftp 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit udp object-group rasvpn-infra object-group fw-admins eq tftp 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit tcp object-group rasvpn-infra object-group tacacs-servers eq tacacs 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit icmp object-group rasvpn-infra any object-group grp-icmp 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit udp object-group rasvpn-ica object-group intranet-wins eq netbios-ns 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit ip 172.16.0.152 255.255.0.0 any 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit ip 172.16.0.154 255.255.255.0 any 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit ip 172.16.0.192 255.255.255.0 any 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit ip 172.16.0.193 255.255.255.0 any 
example8-list rasvpn-1 deny tcp any any object-group grp-nbt 
example8-list rasvpn-1 deny udp any any object-group grp-nbt 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit ip object-group rasvpn-emp object-group dmz-networks 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit ip object-group rasvpn-emp 192.0.2.70 255.255.255.0 
example8-list rasvpn-1 permit tcp object-group rasvpn-ica object-group Ica-ftp-Server eq ftp
